 ) The symbol of capitalism, Hong Kong, is constantly skyrocketing, as if saying that my building is taller than yours
 real estate kaa matlab ab pahadiyon se ghira vah bangala nahin he, jiske sunahare daravaaje aupniveshik thasak main band rahaa karte the
 Now real estate means such a skyscraper, which she is paying for the work, which she claims all her fraternity around the world, but never achieved
 yah oonchai akaash chuumati he
 Hong Kong was the second city of the British Raj
 kalakatta pehla tha
 It is evident that being the capital of the British Empire, the wheel of fortune of the empire also revolved from here
 angrejon ne sabase badi galati yah kii ki 1911 main apni satta kaa centre vahaan se hataakar dilli le aae
 It took more than a decade to reach Delhi and within two decades of coming here, the empire which had stood in two centuries had gone by hand
 1947 tak aate-aate laga ki angrejon ko lautne main badi raahat mahasoos ho rahi thi
 Obviously, as much as India was a colony, it was equally responsible
 kalakatta yadi angrejon kii jarurat thi to honkong unka shauk tha, jise ve kisi keemat par khona nahin chaahate the
 i can only guess what the reasons were
 kalakatta mahaj rajdhani thi, jabaki honkong aiyashi kaa adda
 The British were compelled to live together in Calcutta
 lekin tanaav dhire-dhire badhata gaya kyonki unheen angrejon kii di hui shiksha ne na chaahate hue bhi hindustaniyon kii mahatvakankshaon ko jagaa diya
 In Hogkang, the British could live separately and systematically meet all their metropolitan needs, which were dear to them
 masalan club cameti ke chunaav
 Hindustan now needed such elite people who would have kept the front door open to the elite, but would have allowed the traders to come through the back door
 bharat kii puraani sattayen is dhoortta kaa istemaal karnaa jaanati thim
 But Mandarin-speaking Chinese did not need to have social or any kind of relationship with the British who were in selling currency and buying shares
 apiumkhor bhi yahaan opium bechney vaale ke prati anmana ravaiya rakhata tha, baavjood iske ki yah dhimaa jehar apane prati dhikkaar or angrejon ke prati dwesh kaa bhav paidaa karata tha
 China saw both good and bad rulers, but it was a new type of rule - the rule of hallucinations
 maotse tung ne china kii seemaa ko pashchim main tibet tak pahunchaa diya lekin apane purab main is chote se dweep ko lekar kaaphi chaukann rahe
 According to his ideology, Mao did not need hongkong
 lekin unke uttaradhikari deng jiyaoping ko isaki jarurat thi
 History has changed the situation so that anyone would be embarrassed
 deng ne china ko khandaani dhandha banane se bachaa liya or use ek communist korporation main tabdeel kar daalaa
 It cleverly defeated this obstinate ideology by showing a mirror of prosperity
 honkong ab kalank nahin rah gaya tha, vah prerana tha
 At a time when China's per capita income was $ 300 and Hong Kong's $ 10,000, Deng opened China's doors and changed the world
 deng ne maao ke kader or sangharsh ke nuskhe kii jagah kaabiliyat or sthirataa ko sthapit kiya
 He set a new objective for the new Mandarin bureaucracy: popular welfare work according to the wishes of the people
 is kalyaan kaa laabh paane ke liye unhone chaar saamaajik tabake tay kiye, jo aaj tak chalan main hai
 The highest rung was dominated by the Mandarin, a clan accustomed to rule

 At the third place was the Achachachaya middle class, who saw their ancestors being punished and humiliated during the Cultural Revolution
 is tabake ne deng ke saamaajik ganit ko saharsha gale lagaaya, jo uske liye ascharyajanak dhang se acchhee kismat lekar aayaa tha
 In the last or leftover space, the marginalized poor were kept
 yah spes lagaataar badhaai jaani thi

 isane na sirf chini samaaj main nayakon or khalnaayakon kii ek bemail khichdi pakaa daali, balki raaj karne ke mandaarinon ko mili divine adhikaar ko chunauti dene vaala dussahas bhi paidaa kar diya
 Hong Kong did not succumb to Beijing after the return of the British, but emerged as a courageous leader of democracy
 china kii satta ne poonjeevaad ko badi aasaani se pachaa liya tha, lekin vah honkong ko nahin pachaa paa rahaa he

 sabar mandaarinon kaa gun he
